<name>Jim Collins< /name><Date>1372708679033< /Date><rating>2<//rating>< Review>
Normally the service is excellent here - usually much better than the one combined with A&W at Mitchell and Hatch, but not so much this time.

I ordered the 8-piece meal. For starters, I was told they were completely out of the cole slaw. Really?! KFC's cole slaw is as much a signature item as their chicken. I should have just left then, but I was hungry for the chicken.

I had to wait quite a while for the order as they apparently did not have any corn ready. But it eventually was done and I got my order. I was pretty surprised when I got home to find that I was ripped off on the meal. Normally an 8-piece meal includes two of each: breast, wing, thigh, and drumstick. Instead, with this order I got zero breasts, 1 thigh, 5 (FIVE?!) drumsticks, and 2 wings.

Also, minor but also indicative of things - the corn normally comes on a stick, these did not.

Since I did not see a manager (I know the usual one well and he normally does a good job), I have to assume that since it was after 8, they were in the "getting off work soon" mode of operation and didn't really care about good customer service.

So buyer beware if it's getting a little late here.</Review>

<review>Before my most recent visit, it had been years since I've been here. I am a DDD and that has always proven to be problematic. I've hated bra shopping because of it, however, Victoria Secret has really changed how they do things.
I went in, got measured and was sent straight to the dressing room (nothing in hand besides my card). They had me try on a bra in my measurement and confirmed it was a comfortable fit. From there I was given 4 different styles of bras based on what I was looking for. Once I had picked out the bras I liked they wrote down the styles and my sales lady took me around the store so I could pick out what color I wanted in each.
I bought 4 bras (unheard of for me) and it was so painless. I love each one of them, even the strapless. And none of them are bulky or unflattering. I haven't felt this good in awhile.
Only downside, it was crazy busy and most of my time was spent in a queue.<//review><Pictures>None<//Pictures><Resp>None</Resp><gmap_id>0x809ada1ed4185189:0xb183d147d39f5649</gmap_id></record>
